Abandoned Waterfront
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18

48-65
•
71-100

No

Burrwitch Estates
Burrwitch Village
Festering Lair
Quests:
None
Abandoned Waterfront
is a world area in
Act 1
. It  connects to
Burrwitch Estates
,
Burrwitch Village
and the
Festering Lair
.

CATEGORIES: Locations

The first act of
Grim Dawn
is set in the swamps and backwaters of Burrwitch. The main town is
Devil's Crossing
.

Grim Dawn's Act 2 is set in the ancient ruins of Old Arkovia and involves dealing with the threat to Devil's Crossing posed by
Cronley's Gang
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 3
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_3
======================================================================

Act 3 involves reaching Homestead and dealing with both the food shortage and the threats posed by the Aetherials and Chthonians.

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 4
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_4
======================================================================

Act 4 takes place in the mountainous region of Asterkarn and sees the final showdown between the Black Legion and the Chthonic forces.

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 5
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_5
======================================================================

The fifth act of
Grim Dawn
is available only with the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is set in the Forests north of
Burrwitch Village
.
Act 5 Quests

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 6
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_6

The sixth act of
Grim Dawn
is available only with the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is set in the city of Malmouth.

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 7
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_7
======================================================================

Act 7 is available with the
Forgotten Gods
Expansion and takes place in the distant land of the Korvan Basin. Although it can be accessed after killing the
Warden
at the end of
Act 1
, there are story and lore elements which place it after the other six acts.
The story chapter begins by talking to the
Emissary
, who can be found outside
Devil's Crossing
,
Homestead
,
Fort Ikon
,
Coven's Refuge
or
Sewer Hideout
. He will open a permanent portal to the Act 7 town hub, the
Conclave of the Three
.

Burial Hill
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
4-7
•
5-65
•
6-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Lower Crossing
The Burial Cave
The Old Dump
Quests:
None
Burial Hill
is a world area in
Act 1
. It has connects to
Lower Crossing
and
The Old Dump
. The area also features the entrances to
The Burial Cave
.

Burrwitch Cathedral
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
35-50
•
40-74
•
50-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
East Marsh
Quests:
N/A
Burrwitch Cathedral is a world area in
Act 1
added by the
Forgotten Gods
Expansion. It connects to
East Marsh
and is accessed by crossing the bridge in the north-east of the Marsh.
The area is infested with
Chthonian
Cultists and monsters.
Interests

Burrwitch Estates
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Abandoned Waterfront
Burrwitch Village
The Warden's Cellar
Gloomwald
Quests:
None
Burrwitch Estates
is a world area
Act 1
. It connects to
Burrwitch Village
and the
Abandoned Waterfront
, and contains entrances to
Dank Cellar
,
Musty Cellar
and
The Warden's Cellar
. A bridge in the northeast connects to
Gloomwald
, the first area of the
Ashes of Malmouth
.
Interests
Desecrated Shrine
(Normal/Elite)

Burrwitch Outskirts
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
46-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
The Flooded Passage
Foggy Bank
Burrwitch Village
Quests:
Tale of Two Blacksmiths
The Ironclad Chef
Burrwitch Outskirts
is an world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
The Flooded Passage
, the
Foggy Bank
and
Burrwitch Village
.
The area also contains entrances to
Depraved Sanctuary
,
Smuggler's Basin
,
The Burial Cave
and
Flooded Cellar
.

Burrwitch Village
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Abandoned Waterfront
Burrwitch Estates
Mud Row
Quests:
A Cultist in the Midst
Burrwitch Village
is a world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
Burrwitch Outskirts
,
Burrwitch Estates
,
Abandoned Waterfront
and
Mud Row
.
The area also contains entrances to
Flooded Cellar
and the
Infested Cellar
.

Cavern
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
8-12
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Foggy Bank
Quests:
None
Note: There are multiple Cavern areas. Please see
Cavern
for a list.
Cavern
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It has two entrance/exits in
Foggy Bank
.
The area is home to
Primordian, the Forgotten One
, a unique Slith Boss.

Cavern
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
7-14
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Wightmire
Quests:
A Rover Rescue
Note: There are multiple Cavern areas. Please see
Cavern
for a list.
This
Cavern
is a small underground world area in
Act 1
. It has one entrance/exit, with three possible spawn point locations around
Wightmire
.
The cavern contains some
Convict
enemies and a small side quest.
Interests
Dirt-Covered Note
Ornate Strongbox
Untouched Meal

A Rover Rescue

======================================================================
PAGE: Challenge dungeon
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Challenge_dungeon
======================================================================

Challenge dungeons
are areas in
Grim Dawn
that contain some of the most difficult content of the game, and are intended to provide the player with a means to test their skills, as well as additional end-game and farming options. Numerous side-areas fall into this category, as well as the special "rogue-like" dungeons.
Rogue-like dungeons
At the pinnacle of challenge dungeons are "rogue-like" dungeons, which are named after the early predecessor of the modern action-RPG genre called "Rogue (1985)" . Rogue-likes are characterized by random layouts and permanent death that made the experience intense, and final victory all the more satisfying. Unless playing a hardcore character, death is not permanent in
Grim Dawn
, but
Crate
have tried to capture the thrill of rogue-likes in these special challenge dungeons by sealing the door upon entering and disabling
riftgates
so that there is no way out except by death or reaching the end.
A crafted
Skeleton Key
is required to unlock the door to a rogue-like dungeon each time the player enters. These dungeons are populated by various traps and numerous unique enemy heroes and bosses. Layout is also partially randomized, so that the player may not be able to take the same way through as the previous time, and treasures may not appear in the same locations.
There are five different rogue-like dungeons for the player to explore, each with their own theme and monster faction.
Steps of Torment
Main article:
Steps of Torment
The first challenge dungeon, the
Steps of Torment
, can be accessed in
Act 2
, with the entrance located in the
Broken Hills
. Populated by the
Undead
, this dungeon consists of 5 levels. Level 4 and 5 make up the rogue-like section.
Port Valbury
Main article:
Port Valbury
Port Valbury is found in
Act 3
. It is accessed via an Aetherial Rift that is located beyond the
Detonation Site
in
The Conflagration
. This dungeon is an above-ground zone over-run with
Aetherials
.
Bastion of Chaos
Main article:
Bastion of Chaos
Found at the end of
Act 4
, the Bastion of Chaos entrance located in the
Necropolis Interior
. Populated entirely by
Chthonians
, the dungeon has four levels, with levels 2 to 4 comprising the rogue-like section.
Ancient Grove
Main article:
Ancient Grove
The Ancient Grove is found in the southeast corner of
Ugdenbog
in
Act 5
. It is populated by
Beasts
. A
Skeleton Key
is required to enter the
Feral Thicket
and progress to the
Tainted Wood
.
Tomb of the Heretic
Main article:
Tomb of the Heretic
The Tomb of the Heretic is accessed via the
Lost Oasis
in
Act 7
. It consists of three levels, with a skeleton key required to access the final two. The
Paying Debts
quest leads the player to the tomb, but is not required to access it.

Conclave of the Three
Location Info
Act:
7
Monster
Levels:
15-75
•
25-90
•
30-120

Yes
Adjacent:
Shrine of Horran
Forgotten Cellar
The Veiled Den
The Shattered Realm
Korvan Plateau
Quests:
Many
The Conclave of the Three is an area in
Act 7
, and the main town and quest hub for
Forgotten Gods
Expansion content.
Interests
Witch God Bounty Table
Rift Gate

Convergence of the Covenant

- secret area with access immediately south of the Riftgate. An
Urn Cluster
contains the
Totally Normal Shield
Legendary item.
Cellar Door - hidden behind
Reida - Wares of Dreeg
, leads to the
Forgotten Cellar
.

Convict's Tunnel
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
7-14
•
9-68
•
11-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Devil's Crossing
Prison Dungeons
Quests:
None
Convict's Tunnel
is a small underground world area in
Act 1
. It connects to
Devil's Crossing
and the
Prison Dungeons
.
The tunnel can be accessed by a Trap Door located Devil's Crossing and unlocked during the
And Not a Drop to Drink
side quest.

Cultist's Lair
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
9-13
•
46-60
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Foggy Bank
Quests:
A Sacrifice
The
Cultist's Lair
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It is accessed by a Trap Door inside a house in the
Foggy Bank
. The Trap Door is unmarked on the world Map.
Interests
Missive to Wightmire Bloodbound
Quests
A Sacrifice
NPCs
Isaac

Bloodsworn Adulant

Dank Cellar
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Estates
Quests:
None
Dank Cellar
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It has three entrances in
Burrwitch Estates
.
Interests
Darlet
Ornate Strongbox
Breakable Wall - secret room contains an Untouched Meal and some small chests.
Treasure Trove
(Elite/Ultimate difficulty)

======================================================================
PAGE: Depraved Sanctuary
CATEGORIES: Act 1 Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Depraved_Sanctuary
======================================================================

Depraved Sanctuary
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
18-40
•
55-65
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Quests:
None
Depraved Sanctuary
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. The area is a challenging dungeon located east of the
Burrwitch Outskirts
riftgate. It is inhabited by large numbers of
Bloodsworn
cultists and their
chthonic
minions.
Entry is gained by means of a locked iron door; to unlock it you must be in possession of the
Strange Key
, which can be obtained in two ways:
As a reward when allowing
Direni
to live in the quest
A Cultist in the Midst
.
As a random drop from cultists in the area (guaranteed from the hero cultist who has a chance of spawning in the Southern most area of the base) or in the
Cultist's Lair
.
Interests
Untouched Meal
One-Shot Chest
Ornate Strongbox
Grand Chest
Salazar, Blade of Ch'thon
(Boss)
Caspis, The Blooddrinker
(Bounty spawn only)

======================================================================
PAGE: Detonation Site
CATEGORIES: Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Detonation_Site
======================================================================

Detonation Sites are places you can use
Dynamite
to remove a roadblock or uncover a cave entrance. Doing so allows access to more areas.

This article is about the location. For the faction that currently inhabits it, see
Devil's Crossing (faction)
.
Devil's Crossing
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
1-4
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Lower Crossing
Convict's Tunnel
Arkovian Foothills
Old Grove
Quests:
Many
Devil's Crossing
is a world area in
Act 1
, and where every character begins the game.
The area is made up of an old Prison where various human survivors of the Grim Dawn have taken refuge. The inside of the prison, along with a few outlying buildings, makes up the starting town and central point from which the wider world of
Cairn
can be explored.
Lore
"I was a prisoner here back when this place still served as an actual prison. When the world went down the slith hole, I stayed here with a few others; it was the safest place I could think of. Clearly Bourbon thought the same when he showed up with the rest of the survivors. Things escalated quickly. I'm sure it was us who fired first, but it was them that fired the last. Those prisoners that survived were driven out and 'set free'. Now call me a coward for all I care, but I hid when the fighting got ugly. Came out later looking like another refugee and no one was the wiser. Never could forgive Bourbon for what he did to us though." -
Direni
Interests
Riftgate
Bridge Repair Site
Crudely Scrawled Note
NPCs
Devil's Crossing is home to a number of
NPCs
who can provide services and
quests
for the player. Some are located in Devil's Crossing at the beginning of the game, while others need to found or rescued in other areas of the game world.

East Marsh
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
35-50
•
60-70
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Mud Row
Craig's Crags
Quests:
None
The
East Marsh
is a world area in
Act 1
. it is a large side area that connects to
Mud Row
and
Craig's Crags
.
Although located in Act 1, it is usually necessary to have completed at least some of
Act 2
to access as
Dynamite
is required to clear debris (Dynamite drops in Act 1 are possible, but very rare), and then 10
Scrap
and 8000 Iron Bits are required to repair the bridge.

Edge of Reality
Location Info
Act:
4
Monster
Levels:
36-60
•
65-70
•
80-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Sanctum of the Immortal
Quests:
No
The Edge of Reality is a world area in
Act 4
. It connects to the
Sanctum of the Immortal
.
The area is a hidden easter-egg on Ultimate difficulty only, and is accessed by completing the
secret quest
relating to
Daila Thornsbury
and her sword
Stormheart
.
The player encounters various creatures including Trolls, Trogs, Aether Corruptions, Dermapterans and Chthonics before reaching the final Boss room.
Interests
Clone's Trove (2)
NPCs
John Bourbon
Creatures
Clone of John Bourbon
Burning Clone of John Bourbon
Frozen Clone of John Bourbon
Electrified Clone of John Bourbon
Tainted Clone of John Bourbon
Deathly Clone of John Bourbon
Corrupted Clone of John Bourbon
The Final Form of the Clone of John Bourbon
The Actually Final Form of the Clone of John Bourbon
Trivia
The Clone of John Bourbon is an in-joke dating back to the Early Access period of development. Prior to the game's completion, when the player came to the end of existing content they would encounter the Clone of John Bourbon, an NPC who would inform the player they had completed all current content and could go no further.

======================================================================
PAGE: Edge of Reality (Act 6)

Edge of Reality
Location Info
Act:
6
Monster
Levels:
n/a
•
n/a
•
80-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Sanctum of the Chosen
Crucible of the Dead
Quests:
none
The Edge of Reality is a
secret area
in
Act 6
.
The area is a hidden easter-egg on Ultimate difficulty only, and is accessed by completing
Lokarr's Secret Quest
.
The Area contains a secret path leads to the
Root of All Evil
, which when defeated will open an Aetherial Rift to the
Sanctum of the Chosen
.
Interests
Clone's Trove
Rift-Claimed Adherent
- there are four such Hero Creatures in the area, each one dropping a different piece of the
Dark One's Gift
item set. (In order,  head, chest, hand and shoulder pieces.)
NPCs
Not a Clone of John Bourbon
Creatures
Root of All Evil
Rift-Claimed Adherent

Festering Lair
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
18-23
•
52-65
•
73-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Abandoned Waterfront
Quests:
None
The
Festering Lair
is a small underground world area in
Act 1
. The entrance is located in the
Abandoned Waterfront
.
Beware the toxic water!

One-Shot Chest
.

Foggy Bank
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
8-12
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Wightmire
Sodden Hollow
Burrwitch Outskirts
The Flooded Passage
Quests:
The Lost Caravan
The
Foggy Bank
is a world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
Wightmire
,
Sodden Hollow
,
Burrwitch Outskirts
and
The Flooded Passage
.
The area contains entrances to the
Cultist's Lair
and a
Cavern
. There is also a broken bridge that can be repaired for 3 scrap and 5000 iron bits to reach Burrwitch Outskirts, or alternatively the Flooded Passage can be taken.
Interests
Journeyman's pack
Isaac's Stash
Ornate Strongbox
Bridge Repair Site

The Lost Caravan

Luther Graves

Hallowed Hill
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
18-40
•
55-65
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
River Passage
Quests:
None
Hallowed Hill
is a "secret" world area in
Act 1
, and is accessed through the
River Passage
.
To find the entrance, head northeast from
Burrwitch Village
Riftgate until you cross the large bridge leading to
Burrwitch Estates
. As soon as you cross the bridge, turn left down the small steps and double back under the bridge. If the steps are blocked you will have to go through the house nearby. The unmarked cave entrance can be found just after passing under the bridge.

Ornate Strongbox
One-Shot Chest

Hargate's Isle
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
6-9
•
8-65
•
10-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Lower Crossing
Hargate's Laboratory
Quests:
None
Hargate's Isle
is a world area in
Act 1
. It is a small island accessed by clicking on a Rowboat found in
Lower Crossing
.
The isle is infested with large numbers of
Slith
.
Interests
Hargate's Journal - Page 1
Trap Door - can only be opened as part of
The Origin of the Slith
quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: Hargate's Laboratory

Hargate's Laboratory
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
30-50
•
48-76
•
70-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Hargate's Isle
Quests:
None
Hargate's Laboratory
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It can be accessed by a Trap Door on
Hargate's Isle
after accepting
The Origin of the Slith
quest.
The area has two levels and contains large sections of floor covered in poisonous water which can cause damage, likely a byproduct of long-term
Slith
occupation as the species is well-known for poisoning the water sources where they reside. Indeed, this is the species's place of origin, as referenced by the journal entries and
one particular resident
found within.
Interests
Floor 1:
Treasure Trove
Hargate's Journal - Page 2
Hargate's Journal - Page 3
Floor 2:
Hargate's Journal - Page 4
Ornate Strongbox
Supreme Chest
Ellena, the First Slith
- Boss creature
Creatures
Arachnid
:
Dreadweave Arachnid

Hidden Laboratory
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
16-30
•
50-65
•
72-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Underground Transit
Ominous Lair
Quests:
None
Hidden Laboratory
is world area in
Act 1
and contains a
Riftgate
. It is accessible from the
Underground Transit
and has two hidden entrances into the
Ominous Lair
.
The area is divided into several sections:
Living Quarters
,
Inner Laboratory
,
Abandoned Storerooms
and finally the
Underground Jail
, which is home to the Act 1 Boss,
The Warden
.
Interests
Untouched meal
Journal of Inquisitor Creed - 5th Entry
Journal of Inquisitor Creed - 6th Entry
Gethrand's Notes - 1st Entry
Gethrand's Notes - 2nd Entry
Gethrand's Notes - Final Entry
Zanbrandt's Notes

Infested Cellar
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Quests:
None
Infested Cellar is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It has two entrances in
Burrwitch Village
.
Interests
Untouched Meal
There is One Breakable wall here
Treasure Trove
(Elite/Ultimate difficulty)

Lost Survivor
Lower Crossing
is a world area in
Act 1
, the first the player encounters on leaving
Devil's Crossing
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
Devil's Crossing
and
Burial Hill
.

- leads to
The Hidden Path
Row Boat - takes the player to
Hargate's Isle
Untouched Meal

Moldering Fields
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster

12-15

No

Burrwitch Outskirts

Moldering Fields
is a world area in
Act 1
. It is a sub-section of the
Burrwitch Outskirts
.

Mud Row
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Burrwitch Village
East Marsh
Quests:
None
Mud Row
is a world area in
Act 1
. It is a sub-section of
Burrwitch Outskirts
.
The area features a Bridge Repair Site - repairing the bridge costs 1
Dynamite
, 10
Scrap
and 8000 Iron Bits, and allows access to the
East Marsh
and
Craig's Crags
.
Interests
Untouched Meal
Burrwitch Bridge Repair Site

PAGE: Port Valbury Outskirts

Port Valbury Outskirts
Location Info
Act:
3
Monster
Levels:
36-60
•
55-70
•
75-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
The Conflagration
Port Valbury: Foundation
Quests:
none
Port Valbury Outskirts is a world area in
Act 3
, and forms the initial stage of the
Port Valbury
Challenge Dungeon
.
The area is accessed via a rift located in
The Conflagration
. It is inhabited solely by
Aetherials
and
Aether Corruptions
, and has a +2/3/3 creature level offset.
Interests
Note:
The City is Rotting
- drops from the
Herald of the Stars
One-Shot Chest
Creatures
Boss:
Herald of the Stars
Gallery

Port Valbury:Foundation
Location Info
Act:
3
Monster
Levels:
36-60
•
55-70
•
75-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Port Valbury Outskirts
Port Valbury: Old Town
Quests:
none
Port Valbury: Foundation is a world area in
Act 3
, and forms the second level of the
Port Valbury
Challenge Dungeon
.
The area has a +4/5/5 creature level offset.
Interests
A breakable wall in the north-western corner of the brick area.

Port Valbury: High Town
Location Info
Act:
3
Monster
Levels:
36-60
•
55-70
•
75-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Port Valbury: Old Town
Quests:
none
Port Valbury: High Town is a world area in
Act 3
, and forms the fourth and final level of the
Port Valbury
Challenge Dungeon
. Underneath Port Valbury, after you kill Overlord Van Aldritch you can find small location:
Aldritch's Private Quarters
. You can find Katrine over there, who is worry about her daughter Alice.
The area has a +5/6/6 creature level offset.

Location Info

36-60

•

none
Port Valbury: Old Town is a world area in
Act 3
, and forms the third level of the
Port Valbury
Challenge Dungeon
.
The area has a +4/5/5 creature level offset.

Prison Dungeons
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
7-14
•
9-68
•
11-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Convict's Tunnel
Devil's Aquifer
Quests:
None
Prison Dungeons
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It connects to
Convict's Tunnel
and
Devil's Aquifer
.

Putrid Den
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
5-9
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
The Old Dump
Quests:
None
The
Putrid Den
is a small underground world area in
Act 1
. The entrance is unmarked on the map and can spawn in three different locations, each around the
Old Dump
area.
Beware the toxic water!

River Passage
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
16-30
•
50-65
•
72-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Village
Hallowed Hill
Quests:
None
River Passage
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It can be accessed by an unmarked entrance in
Burrwitch Village
and leads to
Hallowed Hill
.

Slith Altar

Sanctum of the Chosen
Location Info
Act:
6
Monster
Levels:
n/a
•
n/a
•
80-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Malmouth Outskirts
Edge of Reality
Quests:
None
The Sanctum of the Chosen is a small secret area only accessible on Ultimate Difficulty.
Entrance is gained as part of
Lokarr's Secret Quest
.
Interests
Ruined Shrine
(requires a
Skeleton Key
)
Note
:
You Are Not Welcome!
Stone Door - directly behind the Shrine, leading to the
Edge of Reality
Gallery

Sanctum of the Immortal
Location Info
Act:
4
Monster
Levels:
36-60
•
65-70
•
80-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Gates of Necropolis
Edge of Reality (Act 4)
Quests:
None
The Sanctum of the Immortal is a small secret area only accessible on Ultimate Difficulty.
Entrance is gained as part of the secret
quest
relating to
Daila Thornsbury
.
Interests
Ruined Shrine
(Ultimate only)
Note
:
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Final Entry
Loose Torch - opens a Chthonic Rift to the
Edge of Reality
Gallery

URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Secret_Areas

Secret
Areas encompass locations with entrances that are concealed or unmarked. Entrances may have multiple spawn points.
Act 1
Cultist's Lair
Depraved Sanctuary
Hallowed Hill
Ominous Lair
Putrid Den
Smuggler's Basin
Sunken Reliquary
Act 3
Benevald - Strange Wares
The Bone Pit
Bloodbriar's Lair
Buried Crypt
Den of the Lost
Shrine of the Forgotten God
Act 4
Lost Tomb of the Damned
Sanctum of the Immortal
Edge of Reality
Act 6
Edge of Reality
In addition, many normal areas, particularly undergrounds, also have secret rooms and passages that can be accessed through breakable walls. These rooms can contain extra loot or monsters. Such areas are listed below and details can be found on the area's individual page.
Infested Cellar
Musty Cellar
Dank Cellar

Underground Transit

Shrine of the
Forgotten God
Location Info
Act:
3
Monster
Levels:
31-45
•
60-70
•
76-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Gryver's Mill
Quests:
None
The
Shrine of the Forgotten God
is a
secret area
in
Act 3
It can be accessed from the bottom corner of
Gryver's Mill
; there is a small waterfall which can be passed under to reach the Shrine.
The Forgotten God in question is
Korvaak
, whose image is depicted on the shrine.
The area is inhabited by a few
manticores
.
Interests
Ancient Sarcophagus
Note:
Scribe Osteram's Notes
Breakable urn cluster:
Totally Normal Bulwark
(Forgotten Gods only)
Creatures
Manticore Blackmane
Manticore Nightstalker
Manticore Alpha

Smuggler's Basin
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
18-40
•
55-65
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Quests:
None
"A presence far more powerful than you dwells in this place..."
Smuggler's Basin
is a semi-secret underground area in
Act 1
. The entrance is unmarked and may spawn in any of three locations around the
Burrwitch Outskirts
and
Mud Row
.
The area contains one monster, a Boss:
Gutworm, the Maneater
.

Supreme Chest
Gallery

Sodden Hollow
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster

7-10

No

Wightmire
Foggy Bank

Sodden Hollow
is a world area in
Act 1
. It connects to
Wightmire
and
Foggy Bank
.

Sunken Reliquary
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
25-48
•
55-70
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
The Flooded Passage
Quests:
None
The
Sunken Reliquary
is a
secret
world area in
Act 1
and connects to
The Flooded Passage
.
Although located in Act 1, it is necessary to have completed at least some of Act 2 to enter, as access is gained by placing 3
Dynamite
in the
Detonation Site
to unblock the entrance.

Temple of the Three
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
35-60
•
60-70
•
74-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
East Marsh
Quests:
n/a
The
Temple of the Three
is a world area in
Act 1
. The dungeon entrance is located in a secret area off the
East Marsh
, and access is unlocked during the
Hidden Path
side quest.
Interests
Ramblings of Ughdar
- Note
The Runes Fall Silent
- Note
Breakable Wall - Second of the four submerged rooms on the north side of map
Breakable Wall - West of the first green seal before the boss room
Breakable Wall - South side of room with the second green seal right before the boss room
Breakable Wall - South of the Attendant in the final room

The Attendant

The Burial Cave
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
12-18
•
48-65
•
71-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Quests:
None
The Burial Cave
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. Not to be confused with the Burial Cave near Devil's Crossing, it has two entrances in the
Burrwitch Outskirts
.

The Burial Cave
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
4-7
•
5-65
•
6-120
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Burial Hill

The Burial Cave
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It has two entrances on
Burial Hill
.

The Flooded Passage
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
9-13
•
46-60
•
71-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Foggy Bank
Burrwitch Outskirts
Sunken Reliquary
Quests:
None
The Flooded Passage
is an underground world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
Foggy Bank
and the
Burrwitch Outskirts
.
The exit to Burrwitch Outskirts is blocked until you defeat the
Ancient Shambler
boss.
Interests
Desecrated Shrine
(Normal only)
Detonation Site
- requires 3 Dynamite; unblocks the entrance to the
Sunken Reliquary
Slith Altar
Creatures
Boneback
Boneback Gnasher

Rabid Boneback
Scavenger

The Warden's Cellar
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
15-25
•
50-65
•
72-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
Burrwitch Estates
Underground Transit
Quests:
None
The Warden's Cellar
is world area in
Act 1
. It is accessible from
Burrwitch Estates
.
Specifically from the rear of the Warden's mansion.
The area contains several breakable walls and secret areas.
Interests
Untouched meal
Ornate Strongbox
Creatures
Aether Corruption
:
Corruption
Overseer
Overmind
Walking Dead
Wretcher
Burning Dead
Plague Walker
Fury
Cold One
Rotting Soldier

Underground Jail
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
16-30
•
50-65
•
72-100
Riftgate:
No
Adjacent:
Hidden Laboratory
Inner Laboratory
Quests:
None
The
Underground Jail
is a world area in
Act 1
and is the final section of the
Hidden Laboratory
. This area contains the final Act 1 boss,
The Warden
.

Underground Transit
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
16-30
•
50-65
•
72-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
The Warden's Cellar
Hidden Laboratory
Quests:
None
The
Underground Transit
is a world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
The Warden's Cellar
and the
Hidden Laboratory
.
The area contains several breakable walls and secret areas, and an
Abandoned Storerooms
section.

(Normal/Elite/Ultimate)

Wightmire
Location Info
Act:
1
Monster
Levels:
5-9
•
45-60
•
70-100
Riftgate:
Yes
Adjacent:
The Old Dump
Sodden Hollow
Foggy Bank
Quests:
That Good Old Slith Charm
Wightmire
is a world area in
Act 1
. It has a
Riftgate
and connects to
The Old Dump
,
Sodden Hollow
and
Foggy Bank
.
The area consists of a large area of marshland that lies east of
Devil's Crossing
.
Wightmire features a small Rover camp with several NPCs, including a merchant who will buy equipment at a higher rate than in Devil's Crossing.
Interests
Cavern
Cavern
Journeyman's Pack

That Good Old Slith Charm
